Calculate threshold above which the excess should create a new swarm. The threshold should be such that
\begin{DoxyEnumerate}
\item there is enough excess to create a new swarm of size N\+E\+W\+\_\+\+S\+W\+A\+R\+M\+\_\+\+S\+I\+ZE A\+ND
\item there is enough excess to leave I\+D\+E\+A\+L\+\_\+\+S\+W\+A\+R\+M\+\_\+\+M\+A\+R\+G\+IN excess in the existing swarms

{\footnotesize\ttfamily constexpr uint16\+\_\+t service\+\_\+nodes\+::pulse\+\_\+validator\+\_\+bit\+\_\+mask (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}{ }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [constexpr]}}

\mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceservice__nodes_ace17ff5e64e8f1177aa11e824a7d2756}\label{namespaceservice__nodes_ace17ff5e64e8f1177aa11e824a7d2756}} 
\index{service\_nodes@{service\_nodes}!quorum\_checksum@{quorum\_checksum}}
\index{quorum\_checksum@{quorum\_checksum}!service\_nodes@{service\_nodes}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{quorum\_checksum()}{quorum\_checksum()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily uint64\+\_\+t service\+\_\+nodes\+::quorum\+\_\+checksum (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{const std\+::vector$<$ \mbox{\hyperlink{structcrypto_1_1public__key}{crypto\+::public\+\_\+key}} $>$ \&}]{pubkeys,  }\item[{size\+\_\+t}]{offset = {\ttfamily 0} }\end{DoxyParamCaption})}

Calculates a checksum value from the (ordered!) set of pubkeys to casually test whether two quorums are the same. (Not meant to be cryptographically secure).

offset is used to add multiple lists together without having to construct a separate vector, that is\+: \begin{DoxyVerb}checksum([a,b,c,d,e])
\end{DoxyVerb}


and \begin{DoxyVerb}checksum([a,b,c]) + checksum([d,e], 3)
\end{DoxyVerb}


yield the same result. Public keys may be null; pubkeys that are skipped via the offset are equivalent to a null pubkey for skipped entries, and the checksum of \mbox{[}a,b,Z\+E\+RO\mbox{]} is equal to the checksum of \mbox{[}a,b\mbox{]} but not equal to \mbox{[}a,Z\+E\+RO,b\mbox{]}. \mbox{\Hypertarget{namespaceservice__nodes_ae274e677a4db6f580c08096ce2b84d89}\label{namespaceservice__nodes_ae274e677a4db6f580c08096ce2b84d89}} 
\index{service\_nodes@{service\_nodes}!quorum\_for\_serialization\_to\_quorum\_manager@{quorum\_for\_serialization\_to\_quorum\_manager}}
\index{quorum\_for\_serialization\_to\_quorum\_manager@{quorum\_for\_serialization\_to\_quorum\_manager}!service\_nodes@{service\_nodes}}
\doxysubsubsection{\texorpdfstring{quorum\_for\_serialization\_to\_quorum\_manager()}{quorum\_for\_serialization\_to\_quorum\_manager()}}
{\footnotesize\ttfamily static \mbox{\hyperlink{structservice__nodes_1_1quorum__manager}{quorum\+\_\+manager}} service\+\_\+nodes\+::quorum\+\_\+for\+\_\+serialization\+\_\+to\+\_\+quorum\+\_\+manager (\begin{DoxyParamCaption}\item[{\mbox{\hyperlink{structservice__nodes_1_1service__node__list_1_1quorum__for__serialization}{service\+\_\+node\+\_\+list\+::quorum\+\_\+for\+\_\+serialization}} const \&}]{source }\end{DoxyParamCaption})\hspace{0.3cm}{\ttfamily [static]}}
